---

## Summary

Discuss plans for migrating off Airtable/Aerops and building out GrowthX's content production platform, including core functionality, user experience, and data model considerations.

---

## Context

_To be generated by LLM._

---

## Relevance

_To be generated by LLM._

---

## Overview

- Need to migrate off Airtable/Aerops by June 16th deadline; focusing on replicating core production workflows first
- Aiming to build a more streamlined UX for editors that guides them through the content creation process step-by-step
- Planning to create a "content inventory" system to track published content, performance metrics, and opportunities
- Discussing how to model and store contextual information ("artifacts") to improve content quality and consistency

---

## Key Topics

### Current Platform Architecture

  - Using Airtable as project management database and Aerops for workflow automation
  - Challenges with current setup: data spread across tools, lack of learning/improvement over time
  - Need to replicate core functionality while improving UX and adding capabilities

### Content Production Workflow

  - Current process: Ideation \> Assignment creation \> Production \> Staging \> Publishing
  - Want to guide editors through process step-by-step rather than grid view
  - Discussing how to model assignments, production steps, reviews, etc.
  - Considering ways to capture learnings/improvements at each step

### Content Inventory System

  - Proposed system to track all published content, metrics, opportunities
  - Would pull data from sitemap, analytics, SEO tools
  - Allows strategic view of content performance and gaps
  - Critical for demonstrating value to clients

### Contextual Information ("Artifacts")

  - Need way to store/retrieve contextual info like company facts, style guides, personas
  - Discussing how to model different types: facts, preferences, instructions, etc.
  - Want system to learn and suggest improvements over time
  - Exploring ways to dynamically insert relevant context into workflows

### User Experience Considerations

  - Want to move away from grid view for most tasks
  - Discussing guided, step-by-step flow for editors
  - Exploring ways to provide context and instructions inline
  - Considering how to handle reviews, approvals, iterations

### Data Model & Architecture

  - Discussing how to model accounts, projects, assignments, content items
  - Exploring options for storing contextual information
  - Considering how to enable experimentation and learning over time
  - Debating level of customization to allow per client

---

## Action Items

**Marcel Santilli**
- Prepare demo of editor workflow using real data. Walk through assignment creation, production steps w/ team.

**Unassigned**
- Implement toggle for advanced/basic mode in pipeline UI. Hide grid for basic users, show for advanced.
- Export all data from Aerops, store in S3 for backup. Prioritize due to 90-day retention limit.
- Add support for standard auth (non-Google) option for client access.
- Set up test environment w/ one simulated client. Identify bugs, log in Linear for team to address.

**Daniel Lopes**
- Design content inventory screen. Include URL input, data pulling, enrichment capabilities.

**Felipe Lima**
- Develop UI for global/project-level context settings. Implement env vars, no UI yet. Enable manual artifact creation/editing.

---
